Cocoon Cleaning Summary 🤗


📃 1. Table Summary


The table shows real estate data for New York City. It includes metrics like inventory (the number of rental listings), prices cut (the exact middle price cut as a percentage of total asking price), Sale-to-List Price Ratio (the final recorded sales price of a home divided by its initial asking price), etc. Data is split by property type (all, condo, coop, SFR). It covers rental data too. Metrics are tracked monthly from 2010 to 2018. Areas are divided into Manhattan submarkets.
